It is an awesome gui based on this ([http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=35087](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=35087))  that can have its own gui or be ran in a terminal.  Written entirely in shell script.

wow. what malls have you been to. In retrospect: theres no Home Depot section or Best Buy in a mall! LIES!

```
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ sudo apt-get install homedepot
[sudo] password for crazyness003: 
Reading package lists... Done
Building dependency tree       
Reading state information... Done
E: Couldn't find package homedepot
```hang on.
```
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ mkdir /home_depot
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ cd home_depot
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ sudo wget http://www.thats-not-in-a-binary.orly/oh_here_it_is/source/home_depot.tgz
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ tar xvpfz home_depot.tgz -C
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ cd home_depot
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ ./configure
*<snip>*
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ make
*<snip>*
crazyness003@the-friggin-mall:~$ makeinstall
*<snip>*
```There. Now we have a Home depot...i think

### Post by crazyness003 on 2009-01-10
```
mkdir /crazyness_tank
cp /tank-maker/source/tank ~/crazyness_tank
cp /tank-maker/source/tank_ammo ~/crazyness_tank
cp /tank-maker/source/tank_fuel ~/crazyness_tank
cd /crazyness_tank
./configure
*<snip>*
make
*<snip>*
sudo makeinstall
*<snip>*
There is a tank waiting in front of Macy's. Thank you for using Tank Maker 2010! Enjoy the chaos!
```Yay! DIBBS! Go make your own tanks now!

### Post by smartboyathome on 2009-01-31
All those can be answered with two simple words: parallel universes. Since you change reality, aren't you just splitting the universe into two different universes, one with that change and one without? So, in theory, you are correct.

Now, I will start sending destruction through the black holes to form quasars! *uses force to throw pieces of destruction into the black holes* :twisted:

---

### Post by crazyness003 on 2009-01-31
> **smartboyathome said:**
> All those can be answered with two simple words: parallel universes. Since you change reality, aren't you just splitting the universe into two different universes, one with that change and one without? So, in theory, you are correct.

Now, I will start sending destruction through the black holes to form quasars! *uses force to throw pieces of destruction into the black holes* :twisted:
you cant split a *uni*verse to create 2 universes. That would be a multiverse. Pluse, what you speak of would still exist on the current plane of existance. What I speak of would exist on a different brane of "the big picture" (for lack of better words). Since each "universe" has multitudes of "parallels", they should in fact equal to infinity. Now take infinity, and multiply it by the five different planes of existance to the ***n***th power (***n***= the number of parallel multiverses in each "universe" contained within that plane of existance). Then take that number and multiply it by the number of total "branes" (which is infinity).

So in essence, you exist (or dont, for that matter) as every possible possibility in at least one of your (non-)existances, at the same time.

So. This would mean that you dont exist, at least once (but as "the big picture" is infinitley^infinity huge, that number should at leased be multiplied by infinity).
You=non-existant

### Post by crazyness003 on 2009-02-07
> **smartboyathome said:**
> Woot! I will try going through it to see where I go. The mall is still dying though. If my calculations are correct, by the 500th post, the mall will be dead. :o
actually, your calculations are flawed. Within the &#8747; expression, after the second limit, you forgot to divide by two. This would impact the end result of the equation by increasing the percent error and thus giving a range of 976 to &#8734;. If the equation is to have an error factor of ±35 depending on the variable speed of the spinning /dev/null relative to the center of the 'verse. This would, in fact mean, that since wormholes are carrying &#8734; mass to the singularity (naked or not...but I prefer to see it all :wink: ) The ejected mass would occupy a space that does not exist, thus existing around the singularity itself, since it exists on all planes, verses and branes. So, what you may hypothesize as an ever increasing "black hole", consuming the mall, it is infact consuming itself in a perpetual matter-energy, energy-matter cycle. Rendinering it insignificant to us, since (unfortunately) we cannot see beyond the gamma ray spectrum with any known instrument. This would be a fuzzy line where a higher power might exist. FSM could scientifically exist, within our own very realm of existance.

### Post by crazyness003 on 2009-02-25
> **snova said:**
> Well, the electronegativity of the free ions present in the neurotransmitters in your cerebral cortex made an increase relative to the change in the valence shells of the innermost electrons partaking in a covalent bond of the antimatter stream of mis-aligned synaptic connections. Unfortunately I doubt the --isolated flag made much difference owing to the volatility of particular bosons generated by photons trapped in fields of weak nuclear forces. Thus I shall attempt to determine whether decreasing the neutrino concentration of the particle stream, or at the very least, increasing the volume of the field, has any ability to negate this effect.
> **snova said:**
> I suspect the efficiency of certain important acid reactions have also been decreased, possibly due to the decreasing ability of orbiting Fermions to form ionic bonds during the Krebs process. It is also conceivable that the quantum nature of the device has entangled crucial substances in the axiom system, disturbing the normal functionality and changing the likely hood of proper reactions among polar covalent molecules. I repeat my recommendation of changing the neutrino concentration or the volume of the quantum field.

Actually, the determinant variable in the sub-atomic process of energy transference is the spin of the outer valence electron sub-structures. In the event that the charge is positive (counter-clockwise) then the field-energy must be increased in order to counter the spinning effects. If it is increased by too much, the resulting effect would diminish the valence spin altogether, creating free-radical electrons, which would split into the elemental quarks, most of which would diminish within the 5th, 6th, and 7th dimensions. This would yield a high-energy output, and cause a chain reaction with the rest of the valence shell electrons. If all go off at the same time, the energy must be used in another manner, either by creating a double of each particle of matter "destroyed" or causing focus-coordinated photons within the ultra-violet range of the spectrum, giving a sort of "x-ray vision" effect to anything observed. Which would undoubtly kill the bearer of such energy.

Now if the valence spin is negative (clockwise) then decreasing the field-energy should counter its effects, unless less (negative) energy is necessary. Unfortunately, reversing the polarity of the field-energy would result in the one firing the quantum-destabilizer to experience the same effects I just explained in the first paragraph. 
SO, in order to achieve the resulting anti-spin threshold, a second quantum-destabilizer must be used on the first, in order to counter its effects on the bearer. And so on.

### Post by jenkinbr on 2009-02-26
```

sudo apt-get install robot
```

*that's gonna take a while, it looks like*

<< 15 minutes later >>

Phew, it's done.

pastes the following into a bash script, stored in ~/bin/ called quantumstablize:
```
#!/bin/bash
## issue warning to anybody nearby
xmessage "Run like the wind - keep at least 100 meters away, or you may be affected!!!"

## Provide time to escape
sleep 300

## Undo the quantum-neutrino-destabiliser command from earlier:
quantum-neutrino-destabiliser --target=bgs100 --exposure=10 --confined --isoloated --reverse-polarity

## exit
exit
```

Now, with that saved,

```

jenkinbr@mall ~/$ chmod +x bin/quantumstablize
jenkinbr@mall ~/$ export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
jenkinbr@mall ~/$ robot-cmd -a -f --command='quantumstablize'

```

*runs like the wind*

And start hogging the shower

Decide to give you a permanent wedgie
Legally change your name to Reggie
Even mess up the pH balance in your pool

And leave a bunch of Twinkie wrappers all over the place

Forward this message on to everybody

Delete immediately before someone gets hurt

Tell everyone you know, tell everybody now

So before it e-mails your grandmother all of your Porn...
